<div class="sastodealinfo">
<h4>Sastodeal: The One-stop Shopping Destination</h4>
<br/>
<p>About Us</p>
<p>Our story began in Dec 2011, when internet penetration in Nepal was just about 9%. Yet, we were encouraged to start not just a company but an ecommerce industry that would have a significant impact in Nepal’s economy for generations to come. Bootstrapped with just Rs.50,000, we rented a small garage, worked on broken furniture and chairs and worked hard to build a strong company and significantly contributing in building an ecommerce industry. Today,  Sastodeal  is one of the leading ecommerce companies in Nepal with millions of customers and thousands of vendors / partners all over Nepal. We have a logistic network that ensures deliveries in most parts of the nation with exceptions of some locations (work in progress). Our goal is to ensure that our users and customers can buy products at affordable prices, get their products delivered as assured, and on time regardless of their location. On the other hand, we provide a platform for our vendors to cater to millions of customers without additional cost to their business.  
</p>
<p>Sastodeal  Vision</p>
<p>
Our vision is to make Nepal proud by being the best local example in customer experience. </p>

<script>
    (function  () {
        require(['jquery', 'js/popper.min', 'js/bootstrap.bundle.min', 'js/owl.carousel.min','js/voiceSearch'], function ($) {
            $(".menu-dropdown-icon a")
                .click(function(e) {
                    var link = $(this);

                    var item = link.parent("li");
                    
                    if (item.hasClass("active")) {
                        item.removeClass("active").children("a").removeClass("active");
                    } else {
                        item.addClass("active").children("a").addClass("active");
                    }

                    if (item.children(".menu-dropdown-icon").length > 0) {
                        var href = link.attr("href");
                        link.attr("href", "#");
                        setTimeout(function () { 
                            link.attr("href", href);
                        }, 300);
                        e.preventDefault();
                    }
                })
                .each(function() {
                    var link = $(this);
                    if (link.get(0).href === location.href) {
                        link.addClass("active").parents("li").addClass("active");
                        return false;
                    }
                });
        });
    })();</script>

<script>
    require([
        'jquery',
        'mage/url'
    ], function (
        $,
        murl
    ) {
        $(document).ready(function () {
            $(".popup-form-submit").submit(function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();

                
                var emptyCount = 0;
                $('.popup-form-submit input').each(function () {
                    var value = $(this).val();
                    if (value === "") {
                        emptyCount = emptyCount + 1;
                    }
                });

                
                var password = $('.popup-form-submit #password').val();
                var confirmPassword = $('.popup-form-submit #password-confirmation').val();
                $('#submit-sign-up').prop("disabled", false)
                if((emptyCount == 0) && (password === confirmPassword) && ($('.help-text').css('color') === "rgb(0, 128, 0)") &&
                    ($(".popup-form-submit .password .password-weak").length == 0)
                 ) {
                    $.ajax({
                        url: murl.build('customer/account/createpost'),
                        type: "POST",
                        data: $('#customer-form-validate').serialize(),
                        showLoader: true,
                        cache: false,
                        success: function (response) {
                            $('.action-close').trigger('click');
                            $('#product-addtocart-button').trigger( "click" );
                            location.reload();
                            return true;
                        }
                    });
                    return false;
                }
            });
        });
    });</script>

<script>
    require(['jquery'], function ($) {
        $('#email_address').focusout(function () {
            var emailVal = $(this).val();
            var emailValUrl = 'https://www.sastodeal.com/sastomarketplace/account/uniquecustomeremail'
            $('#email_address').siblings('.help-text').remove();
            var mailformat = /^\w+([\.-]?\w+)*@\w+([\.-]?\w+)*(\.\w{2,3})+$/;
            if (!emailVal.match(mailformat)) {
                $('#email_address').after('<span class="help-text" style="color:red;">Email is not valid</span>');
                return false;
            }
            $.ajax({
                showLoader: true,
                url: emailValUrl,
                type: 'POST',
                data: {
                    form_key: $.mage.cookies.get('form_key'),
                    email: emailVal
                },
                dataType: 'json',
                beforeSend: function () {
                    $('body').trigger('processStart');
                },
                success: function (response) {
                    $('body').trigger('processStop');
                    if (response.message) {
                        $('#email_address').after('<span class="help-text" style="color:green;">' + response.message + '</span>')
                        $('#submit-sign-up').prop("disabled", false)
                    }
                },
                error: function (error) {
                    $('body').trigger('processStop');
                    if (error.responseJSON != undefined && error.responseJSON.message) {
                        $('#email_address').after('<span class="help-text" style="color:red;">' + error.responseJSON.message + '</span>');
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    });</script>

<script>
        require([
            "jquery",
            "Magento_Ui/js/modal/alert",
            "mage/mage"
        ], function($, alert) {
            var askDataForm = $('#ask-form');
            var cardType = 1;

            askDataForm.mage('validation', {});
            var flagDataForm = $('#flag-form');
            flagDataForm.mage('validation', {});
            if (cardType == 2) {
                $('.product-info-main').before($('#mp-wk-block'));
            } else {
                $('.product-info-main').append($('#mp-wk-block'));
            }
            $('#mp-wk-block').show();

            $('body').append($('#wk-mp-ask-data'));
            $('body').append($('#wk-mp-flag-data'));
            $(".wk-seller-rating-number" ).mouseover(function() {
                $( ".wk-seller-rating" ).show();
            }).mouseout(function() {
                $( ".wk-seller-rating" ).hide();
            });

            $('#askque').click(function() {
                $('#ask-form input,#ask-form textarea').removeClass('mage-error');
                $('.page-wrapper').css('opacity','0.4');
                $('.wk-mp-model-popup').addClass('_show');
                $('#wk-mp-ask-data').show();
            });
            $('.wk-close').click(function() {
                $('.page-wrapper').css('opacity','1');
                $('#resetbtn').trigger('click');
                $('#wk-mp-ask-data').hide();
                $('#ask-form .validation-failed').each(function() {
                    $(this).removeClass('validation-failed');
                });
                $('#ask-form .validation-advice').each(function() {
                    $(this).remove();
                });
            });
            $('#askbtn').click(function() {
                if (askDataForm.valid()!=false) {
                    var thisthis = $(this);
                    if (thisthis.hasClass("clickask")) {
                         thisthis.removeClass('clickask');
                        $('#wk-mp-ask-data').addClass('mail-procss');
                        $.ajax({
                            url:'https://www.sastodeal.com/marketplace/seller/sendmail/',
                            data:$('#ask-form').serialize(),
                            type:'post',
                            dataType:'json',
                            success:function(d) {
                                thisthis.addClass('clickask');
                                $('#wk-mp-ask-data').removeClass('mail-procss')
                                alert({
                                    title: $.mage.__('Success Message'),
                                    content: $.mage.__('Your mail has been sent...'),
                                    actions: {
                                        always: function(){
                                            $('.wk-close,#resetbtn').trigger('click');
                                        }
                                    },
                                    buttons: [{
                                        text: $.mage.__('Close'),
                                        class: 'action primary close',
                                        click: function () {
                                            this.closeModal(true);
                                        }
                                    }]
                                });
                                $('.wk-close,#resetbtn').trigger('click');
                            }
                        });
                         }
                    return false;
                }
            });
            $('#reportflag').click(function() {
                $('#flag-form input,#flag-form textarea').removeClass('mage-error');
                $('.page-wrapper').css('opacity','0.4');
                $('.wk-mp-model-flag-popup').addClass('_show');
                $('#wk-mp-flag-data').show();
            });
            $('.wk-product-flag-close').click(function() {
                $('.page-wrapper').css('opacity','1');
                $('#resetflagbtn').trigger('click');
                $('#wk-mp-flag-data').hide();
                $('#flag-form .validation-failed').each(function() {
                    $(this).removeClass('validation-failed');
                });
                $('#flag-form .validation-advice').each(function() {
                    $(this).remove();
                });
            });
            $('.flag-reason').on('change',function(e) {
                if($(this).val() == "other_value") {
                    $('.wk-flag-other-reason').show();
                    $('.wk-flag-other-reason').addClass('required-entry');
                } else {
                    $('.wk-flag-other-reason').hide();
                    $('.wk-flag-other-reason').removeClass('required-entry');
                }
            });
            $('#resetflagbtn').on('click', function(e) {
                $('.wk-flag-other-reason').show();
                $('.wk-flag-other-reason').addClass('required-entry');
            });
            $('#flagbtn').click(function() {
                if (flagDataForm.valid()!=false) {
                    var thisthis = $(this);
                    if (thisthis.hasClass("clickflag")) {
                        thisthis.removeClass('clickflag');
                        $('#wk-mp-flag-data').addClass('mail-procss');
                        $.ajax({
                            url:'https://www.sastodeal.com/marketplace/product/reportflag/',
                            data:$('#flag-form').serialize(),
                            type:'post',
                            dataType:'json',
                            success:function(content) {
                                var messageContent = $('.wk-alert-modal-content').html();
                                thisthis.addClass('clickflag');
                                $('#wk-mp-flag-data').removeClass('mail-procss')
                                alert({
                                    title: $.mage.__('Report Product'),
                                    content: $('.wk-flag-status-content'),
                                    actions: {
                                        always: function(){
                                            $('.wk-product-flag-close,#resetflagbtn').trigger('click');
                                            $('.wk-flag-other-reason').show();
                                            $('.wk-flag-other-reason').addClass('required-entry');
                                        }
                                    },
                                    buttons: [{
                                        text: $.mage.__('Close'),
                                        class: 'action primary close',
                                        click: function () {
                                            this.closeModal(true);
                                        }
                                    }]
                                });
                                $('.wk-alert-modal-content').append(messageContent);
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    return false;
                }
            });
        });</script>

            productId: 413052        },

<script>
    function remove(itemId, action){
        require(["jquery"],function($){
            if(action == 'add'){
                $('#qty').val(parseInt($('#qty').val()) + 1)
            }
            else if(action == 'remove'){
                if($('#qty').val() != 1)
                    $('#qty').val(parseInt($('#qty').val()) - 1)
            }
        })
    }</script>

                $('#buy-now-guest').attr('disabled', false);
            });
        });
        $('body').on('click', '#buy-now-guest', () => {
            authenticate.showModal();
            sessionStorage.setItem('buy_now', 1);
            $('#buy-now-guest').attr('disabled', false);
            return true;
        });
    });</script>

<script>
  require(['jquery'],function($) {
    $("#city").css("display", "none");
    $("#area").css("display", "none");
    /*City */
    $('li.region').click(function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    var value = $(this).attr('data-value');
    var region = { region: value };
    $.ajax({
          showLoader: true,
          url: 'https://www.sastodeal.com/pincodecheck/pincode/city/',
          data: region,
          type: "POST",
          dataType: 'json'
          }).done(function (data) {
          
          var myJSON = JSON.stringify(data);
           $.each(JSON.parse(myJSON), function(index, value) {
                    $("#city").append($("<li class='city'></li>").attr("data-value",value).text(value));
                    });
                    $("#city").css("display", "block");
                    $("#region").css("display", "none");
                    $("#area").css("display", "none");
                    $(".region_bread").html(value).css('color','#613F99').append('<span> ></span>');
                    $(".city_bread").html("<span style='color: #5b5b5b;'> Select District</span>");
          });
          });
/* Area */
$('body').on('click','.city',function(e){
    e.preventDefault();
    var value = $(this).attr('data-value');
    var city = { city: value };
    $.ajax({
          showLoader: true,
          url: 'https://www.sastodeal.com/pincodecheck/pincode/area/',
          data: city,
          type: "POST",
          dataType: 'json'
          }).done(function (data) {
          
          var myJSON = JSON.stringify(data);


                    $.each(JSON.parse(myJSON), function(index, value) {
                    $("#area").append($("<li class='area'></li>").attr("data-value",value).text(value));
                    });
                    $("#area").css("display", "block");
                    $("#region").css("display", "none");
                    $("#city").css("display", "none");
                    $(".city_bread").html(value).css('color','#613F99').append('<span> ></span>');;
                    $(".area_bread").html("<span style='color: #5b5b5b;'> Select Region</span>");

          });
          });
$('body').on('click','.area',function(e){
    e.preventDefault();
    var value = $(this).attr('data-value');
    var area = { area: value };
    $.ajax({
          showLoader: true,
          url: 'https://www.sastodeal.com/pincodecheck/pincode/all/',
          data: area,
          type: "POST",
          dataType: 'json'
          }).done(function (data) {
          
          var myJSON = JSON.stringify(data);
          var obj=JSON.parse(myJSON);
          $(".selectAddress").css("display", "none");
                    $("#area").css("display", "none");

                    $("#region").css("display", "block");
                    $("#city").css("display", "none");

                    $(".address").html(obj.region + ", " + obj.city + ", " + value);
                    $(".estimate_shipping").html(obj.prepaidcost);
                    $(".estimate_ship, .b_top").css({"display":"block","border-bottom":"1px solid @lighter-gray-x"});
                    $(".b_top").css({"border-bottom":"1px solid @lighter-gray-x", "padding":"10px 0px"});
                    $(".cashdelivery").css("padding","10px 0px");
                    if(obj.iscod == 0)
                    {
                      var codtext ="Cash on Delivery Available";
                    $(".cashdelivery").html(codtext);
                    }
                    $(".city_bread").html(value);
                    $(".region_bread").html("<span style='color: #5b5b5b;'>Select Province</span>");
                    $(".city_bread").html('');
                    $(".area_bread").html('');
                    $(".city").remove();
                    $(".area").remove();
                    console.log(obj.region + ", " + obj.city + ", " + value);
          });
          });


        $('body').on('click','.area',function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
          $(".selectAddress").css("display", "none");
          });
        });</script>

<script>
    require(['jquery'], function ($) {
        $('#reviewBtn').click(function (e) {
            $('.review-add').show();
        });
        var distance = $('.page-main-details').offset().top,
            $window = $(window);

        $window.scroll(function () {
            if ($window.scrollTop() >= distance) {
                $(".prodSticky").addClass("stickyHide");
                $(".stickyHide").removeClass("prodSticky");
                $('.page-main-details').css({'background': '#fafafa', 'z-index': '1'});
            } else {
                $(".stickyHide").addClass("prodSticky");
                $(".prodSticky").removeClass("stickyHide");
                $('.page-main-details').css({'background': '#fafafa', 'z-index': '1'});
            }
        });
        $(".review-items li").hide();
        var size_li = $(".review-items li").size();
        x = 3;
        $('.review-items li:lt(' + x + ')').show();
        $('.allreviewsBtn').click(function () {
            x = (x + 5 <= size_li) ? x + 5 : size_li;
            $('.review-items li:lt(' + x + ')').show();
        });
    });</script>

            $window = $(window);

                $(".stickyHide").removeClass("prodSticky");

<script>
    require([
        'jquery',
        'ibnabmodernizr'
    ], function ($) {
        $( document ).ready(function() {
            $('.menu > ul > li:has( > ul)').addClass('menu-dropdown-icon');
            

            $('.menu > ul > li:has( > ul li)').addClass('megamenu-enabled');
            

            $('.menu > ul > li > ul:not(:has(ul))').addClass('normal-sub');
            

            $(".menu > ul").before("<a href=\"#\" class=\"menu-mobile\">Navigation</a>");

            
            
            
            

            $('.menu > ul > li').hover(function(e) {

                var expanding = $(this);
                
                var timer = window.setTimeout(function () {
                    expanding.data('timerid', null);
                    
                    if ($(window).width() > 943) {
                        expanding.children("ul").stop(true, false).show();
                        e.preventDefault();
                    }

                }, 300);
                
                expanding.data('timerid', timer);
            }, function(e) {

                var timerid = $(this).data('timerid');
                if (timerid != null) {
                    
                    window.clearTimeout(timerid);
                }
                else{
                    $(this).children("ul").hide();
                }
            });

            

            $(".menu > ul > li").click(function () {
                if ($(window).width() <= 943) {
                    $(this).children("ul").fadeToggle(150);
                }
            });
            

            $(".menu-mobile").click(function (e) {
                $(".menu > ul").toggleClass('show-on-mobile');
                e.preventDefault();
            });
        });
    });</script>
